(** ** Definition of displayed pseudofunctor *)

Section DispPseudofunctor.

Context {B₁ : bicat} (D₁ : disp_bicat B₁)
        {B₂ : bicat} (D₂ : disp_bicat B₂)
        (F : psfunctor B₁ B₂).

(** *** Data *)

Definition disp_psfunctor_data : UU
  :=
    ∑ (obFF : ∏ x:B₁, D₁ x → D₂ (F x))
      (morFF : ∏ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁⟦x,y⟧) (xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y),
               (xx -->[f] yy) →
               (obFF x xx -->[#F f] obFF y yy))
      (cellFF : ∏ (x y : B₁) (f g : B₁⟦x,y⟧) (α : f ==> g) (xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y)
                  (ff : xx -->[f] yy) (gg : xx -->[g] yy),
                (ff ==>[α] gg) → (morFF x y f xx yy ff ==>[##F α] morFF x y g xx yy gg))
      (disp_psfunctor_id : ∏ (x : B₁) (xx : D₁ x),
                           disp_invertible_2cell
                             (psfunctor_id F x)
                             (id_disp (obFF x xx))
                             (morFF x x (id₁ x) xx xx (id_disp xx))),
    (∏ (x y z : B₁) (f : x --> y) (g : y --> z)
       (xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y) (zz : D₁ z)
       (ff : xx -->[f] yy) (gg : yy -->[g] zz),
     disp_invertible_2cell
       (psfunctor_comp F f g)
       (comp_disp (morFF x y f xx yy ff) (morFF y z g yy zz gg))
       (morFF x z (f · g) xx zz (comp_disp ff gg))).

Definition make_disp_psfunctor_data
           (obFF : ∏ x:B₁, D₁ x → D₂ (F x))
           (morFF : ∏ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁⟦x,y⟧) (xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y),
                    (xx -->[f] yy) →
                    (obFF x xx -->[#F f] obFF y yy))
           (cellFF : ∏ (x y : B₁) (f g : B₁⟦x,y⟧) (α : f ==> g) (xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y)
                       (ff : xx -->[f] yy) (gg : xx -->[g] yy),
                     (ff ==>[α] gg) → (morFF x y f xx yy ff ==>[##F α] morFF x y g xx yy gg))
           (disp_psfunctor_id : ∏ (x : B₁) (xx : D₁ x),
                                disp_invertible_2cell
                                  (psfunctor_id F x)
                                  (id_disp (obFF x xx))
                                  (morFF x x (id₁ x) xx xx (id_disp xx)))
           (disp_psfunctor_comp : ∏ (x y z : B₁) (f : x --> y) (g : y --> z)
                                    (xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y) (zz : D₁ z)
                                    (ff : xx -->[f] yy) (gg : yy -->[g] zz),
                                  disp_invertible_2cell
                                    (psfunctor_comp F f g)
                                    (comp_disp (morFF x y f xx yy ff) (morFF y z g yy zz gg))
                                    (morFF x z (f · g) xx zz (comp_disp ff gg)))
  : disp_psfunctor_data
  := (obFF,, morFF,, cellFF,, disp_psfunctor_id,, disp_psfunctor_comp).

Definition disp_psfunctor_ob (FFdata : disp_psfunctor_data)
           {x : B₁}
           (xx : D₁ x)
  : D₂ (F x)
  := pr1 FFdata x xx.

Coercion disp_psfunctor_ob : disp_psfunctor_data >-> Funclass.

Section Projections.

Variable (FFdata : disp_psfunctor_data).

Definition disp_psfunctor_mor
           {x y : B₁} {f : B₁⟦x,y⟧} {xx : D₁ x} {yy : D₁ y}
           (ff : xx -->[f] yy)
  : FFdata x xx -->[#F f] FFdata y yy
  := pr12 FFdata x y f xx yy ff.

Definition disp_psfunctor_cell {x y : B₁} {f g : B₁⟦x,y⟧} {α : f ==> g}
           {xx : D₁ x} {yy : D₁ y}
           {ff : xx -->[f] yy} {gg : xx -->[g] yy}
           (αα : ff ==>[α] gg)
  : disp_psfunctor_mor ff ==>[##F α] disp_psfunctor_mor gg
  := pr122 FFdata x y f g α xx yy ff gg αα.

Definition disp_psfunctor_id {x : B₁} (xx : D₁ x)
  : disp_invertible_2cell (psfunctor_id F x)
                          (id_disp (FFdata x xx))
                          (disp_psfunctor_mor (id_disp xx))
  := pr122 (pr2 FFdata) x xx.

Definition disp_psfunctor_comp
           {x y z : B₁} {f : x --> y} {g : y --> z}
           {xx : D₁ x} {yy : D₁ y} {zz : D₁ z}
           (ff : xx -->[f] yy) (gg : yy -->[g] zz)
  : disp_invertible_2cell (psfunctor_comp F f g)
                          (comp_disp (disp_psfunctor_mor ff) (disp_psfunctor_mor gg))
                          (disp_psfunctor_mor (comp_disp ff gg))
  := pr222 (pr2 FFdata) x y z f g xx yy zz ff gg.

End Projections.


B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FFdata: disp_psfunctor_data
psfunctor_data (total_bicat D₁) (total_bicat D₂)

FFdata: disp_psfunctor_data
psfunctor_data (total_bicat D₁) (total_bicat D₂)

(f : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧),
?F₁ a b f · ?F₁ b c g ==> ?F₁ a c (f · g)

 exact (λ x, (F (pr1 x),, FFdata _ (pr2 x))).

D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FFdata: disp_psfunctor_data
∏ a b : total_bicat D₁,
total_bicat D₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ total_bicat D₂
  ⟦ (λ x : total_bicat D₁,
     F (pr1 x),, FFdata (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) a,
  (λ x : total_bicat D₁,
   F (pr1 x),, FFdata (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) b ⟧
 exact (λ x y f, (#F (pr1 f) ,, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f))).

D₁: disp_bicat B₁

(f g : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧),
f ==> g
→ (λ (x y : total_bicat D₁)
   (f0 : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧),
   # F (pr1 f0),, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f0))
    a b f ==>
  (λ (x y : total_bicat D₁)
   (f0 : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧),
   # F (pr1 f0),, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f0))
    a b g
 exact (λ x y f g α, (##F (pr1 α),, disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (pr2 α))).

id₁
  ((λ x : total_bicat D₁,
    F (pr1 x),, FFdata (pr1 x) (pr2 x)) a) ==>

 (f : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧),
 # F (pr1 f),, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f)) a a
  (id₁ a)
 exact (λ x, iso_in_E_weq _ _ (psfunctor_id F (pr1 x),, disp_psfunctor_id FFdata (pr2 x))).

D₁: disp_bicat B₁

(f : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧),
(λ (x y : total_bicat D₁)
 (f0 : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧),
 # F (pr1 f0),, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f0)) a
  b f
· (λ (x y : total_bicat D₁)
   (f0 : total_bicat D₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧),
   # F (pr1 f0),, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f0))
    b c g ==>
(λ (x y : total_bicat D₁)

  c (f · g)
 
B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FFdata: disp_psfunctor_data
x, y, z: total_bicat D₁
f: total_bicat D₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: total_bicat D₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧
∑
i : invertible_2cell
      (pr1
         (# F (pr1 f),,
          disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f))
       · pr1
           (# F (pr1 g),,
            disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 g)))
      (# F (pr1 (f · g))),
disp_invertible_2cell i
  (pr2
     (# F (pr1 f),, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 f)) ;; 
   pr2
     (# F (pr1 g),, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 g)))
  (disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata (pr2 (f · g)))

    exact (psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g),, disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata (pr2 f) (pr2 g)).
Defined.

(** *** Properties *)

Section DispPseudofunctorLaws.

Variable FFdata : disp_psfunctor_data.

Definition disp_psfunctor_id2_law
  : UU
  := ∏ (a b : B₁) (f : a --> b)
       (aa : D₁ a)
       (bb : D₁ b)
       (ff : aa -->[f] bb),
     disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (disp_id2 ff) =
     transportb
       (λ p : # F f ==> # F f, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ==>[p] disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff)
       (psfunctor_id2 F f) (disp_id2 (disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff)).

Definition disp_psfunctor_vcomp2_law : UU
  := ∏ (a b : B₁) (f g h : B₁ ⟦a, b⟧) (η : f ==> g) (φ : g ==> h) (aa : D₁ a)
       (bb : D₁ b) (ff : aa -->[f] bb) (gg : aa -->[g] bb) (hh : aa -->[h] bb)
       (ηη : ff ==>[η] gg) (φφ : gg ==>[φ] hh),
     disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (ηη •• φφ) =
     transportb
       (λ p : # F f ==> # F h, disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ==>[ p] disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata hh)
       (psfunctor_vcomp F η φ) (disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata ηη •• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata φφ).

Definition disp_psfunctor_lunitor_law : UU
  := ∏ (a b : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧) (aa : D₁ a) (bb : D₁ b) (ff : aa -->[ f] bb),
     disp_lunitor (disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff) =
     transportb
       (λ p, _ ==>[p] _)
       (psfunctor_lunitor F f)
       (((disp_psfunctor_id FFdata aa ▹▹ disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff)
           •• disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata (id_disp aa) ff)
          •• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (disp_lunitor ff)).

Definition disp_psfunctor_runitor_law : UU
  := ∏ (a b : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧) (aa : D₁ a) (bb : D₁ b) (ff : aa -->[ f] bb),
     disp_runitor (disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff) =
     transportb
       (λ p, _ ==>[p] _)
       (psfunctor_runitor F f)
       (((disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ◃◃ disp_psfunctor_id FFdata _)
           •• disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata _ _)
          •• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (disp_runitor ff)).

Definition disp_psfunctor_lassociator_law : UU
  :=
    ∏ (a b c d : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧) (g : B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧) (h : B₁ ⟦ c, d ⟧)
      (aa : D₁ a) (bb : D₁ b) (cc : D₁ c) (dd : D₁ d) (ff : aa -->[ f] bb) (gg : bb -->[ g] cc)
      (hh : cc -->[ h] dd),
    ((disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ◃◃ disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata gg hh)
       •• disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata ff (gg;; hh))
      •• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (disp_lassociator ff gg hh) =
    transportb
      (λ p, _ ==>[p] _)
      (psfunctor_lassociator F f g h)
      ((disp_lassociator (disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff) (disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata gg)
                         (disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata hh)
         •• (disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata ff gg ▹▹ disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata hh))
        •• disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata (ff;; gg) hh).

Definition disp_psfunctor_lwhisker_law : UU
  := ∏ (a b c : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧) (g₁ g₂ : B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧) (η : g₁ ==> g₂)
       (aa : D₁ a) (bb : D₁ b) (cc : D₁ c) (ff : aa -->[ f] bb) (gg₁ : bb -->[ g₁] cc)
       (gg₂ : bb -->[ g₂] cc) (ηη : gg₁ ==>[ η] gg₂),
     disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata ff gg₁ •• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (ff ◃◃ ηη) =
     transportb
       (λ p, _ ==>[p] _)
       (psfunctor_lwhisker F f η)
       ((disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ◃◃ disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata ηη)
          •• disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata ff gg₂).

Definition disp_psfunctor_rwhisker_law : UU
  := ∏ (a b c : B₁) (f₁ f₂ : B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧) (g : B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧) (η : f₁ ==> f₂)
       (aa : D₁ a) (bb : D₁ b) (cc : D₁ c)
       (ff₁ : aa -->[f₁] bb)
       (ff₂ : aa -->[f₂] bb)
       (gg : bb -->[g] cc)
       (ηη : ff₁ ==>[ η] ff₂),
     disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata _ _ •• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (ηη ▹▹ gg) =
     transportb
       (λ p, _ ==>[p] _)
       (psfunctor_rwhisker F g η)
       ((disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata ηη ▹▹ _)
          •• disp_psfunctor_comp FFdata _ _).

Definition is_disp_psfunctor : UU
    := disp_psfunctor_id2_law
         × disp_psfunctor_vcomp2_law
         × disp_psfunctor_lunitor_law
         × disp_psfunctor_runitor_law
         × disp_psfunctor_lassociator_law
         × disp_psfunctor_lwhisker_law
         × disp_psfunctor_rwhisker_law.

Definition disp_psfunctor_id2 (H : is_disp_psfunctor) := pr1 H.

Definition disp_psfunctor_vcomp2 (H : is_disp_psfunctor) := pr12 H.


B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FFdata: disp_psfunctor_data
H: is_disp_psfunctor
a, b: B₁
f, g, h: B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
η: f ==> g
φ: g ==> h
aa: D₁ a
bb: D₁ b
ff: aa -->[ f] bb
gg: aa -->[ g] bb
hh: aa -->[ h] bb
ηη: ff ==>[ η] gg
φφ: gg ==>[ φ] hh
transportf
  (λ p : # F f ==> # F h,
   disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata hh)
  (psfunctor_vcomp F η φ)
  (disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (ηη •• φφ)) =
disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata ηη
•• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata φφ


B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FFdata: disp_psfunctor_data
H: is_disp_psfunctor
a, b: B₁
f, g, h: B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
η: f ==> g
φ: g ==> h
aa: D₁ a
bb: D₁ b
ff: aa -->[ f] bb
gg: aa -->[ g] bb
hh: aa -->[ h] bb
ηη: ff ==>[ η] gg
φφ: gg ==>[ φ] hh
transportf
  (λ p : # F f ==> # F h,
   disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata hh)
  (psfunctor_vcomp F η φ)
  (disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (ηη •• φφ)) =
disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata ηη
•• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata φφ

  
B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FFdata: disp_psfunctor_data
H: is_disp_psfunctor
a, b: B₁
f, g, h: B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
η: f ==> g
φ: g ==> h
aa: D₁ a
bb: D₁ b
ff: aa -->[ f] bb
gg: aa -->[ g] bb
hh: aa -->[ h] bb
ηη: ff ==>[ η] gg
φφ: gg ==>[ φ] hh
disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata (ηη •• φφ) =
transportb
  (λ p : # F f ==> # F h,
   disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata ff ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FFdata hh)
  (psfunctor_vcomp F η φ)
  (disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata ηη
   •• disp_psfunctor_cell FFdata φφ)

  apply (disp_psfunctor_vcomp2 H).
Qed.

End DispPseudofunctorLaws.

(** *** Disp pseudofunct *)

Definition disp_psfunctor : UU
  := ∑ FF : disp_psfunctor_data, is_disp_psfunctor FF.

Coercion disp_psfunctor_to_disp_psfunctor_data (FF : disp_psfunctor)
  : disp_psfunctor_data
  := pr1 FF.


B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor
psfunctor_laws (total_psfunctor_data FF)


B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor
psfunctor_laws (total_psfunctor_data FF)

  repeat apply make_dirprod; intro; intros; (use total2_paths_b; [ apply F | apply FF ]).
Qed.

B₂: bicat

F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor
psfunctor (total_bicat D₁) (total_bicat D₂)


B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁

          pr1 (# EF (f,, ff)),

  (λ p : id₁ (F a) · # F f ==> # F f,

     ▹▹ disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff)

   •• disp_psfunctor_cell FF (disp_lunitor ff))

B₁: bicat

D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor_data
HFF: is_psfunctor (total_psfunctor_data FF)
EF:= make_psfunctor (total_psfunctor_data FF) (pr1 HFF)
  (pr2 HFF): psfunctor (total_bicat D₁) (total_bicat D₂)
a, b: B₁
f: B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
aa: D₁ a
bb: D₁ b
ff: aa -->[ f] bb
disp_runitor (disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff) =
transportb
  (λ p : # F f · id₁ (F b) ==> # F f,
   disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff ;; id_disp (FF b bb) ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff)
  (psfunctor_runitor F f)
  (((disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff
     ◃◃ disp_psfunctor_id FF bb)
    •• disp_psfunctor_comp FF ff (id_disp bb))
   •• disp_psfunctor_cell FF (disp_runitor ff))

    
B₁: bicat
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
B₂: bicat
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor_data
HFF: is_psfunctor (total_psfunctor_data FF)
EF:= make_psfunctor (total_psfunctor_data FF) (pr1 HFF)
  (pr2 HFF): psfunctor (total_bicat D₁) (total_bicat D₂)
a, b: B₁
f: B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
aa: D₁ a
bb: D₁ b
ff: aa -->[ f] bb
P:= ! fiber_paths (psfunctor_runitor EF (f,, ff)): pr2
  (((# EF (f,, ff) ◃ psfunctor_id EF (b,, bb))
    • psfunctor_comp EF (f,, ff) (id₁ (b,, bb)))
   • ## EF (runitor (f,, ff))) =
transportf
  (λ x : pr1 (# EF (f,, ff) · id₁ (EF (b,, bb))) ==>
         pr1 (# EF (f,, ff)),
   (λ η : pr1 (# EF (f,, ff) · id₁ (EF (b,, bb))) ==>
          pr1 (# EF (f,, ff)),
    pr2 (# EF (f,, ff) · id₁ (EF (b,, bb))) ==>[
    η] pr2 (# EF (f,, ff))) x)
  (base_paths (runitor (# EF (f,, ff)))
     (((# EF (f,, ff) ◃ psfunctor_id EF (b,, bb))
       • psfunctor_comp EF (f,, ff) (id₁ (b,, bb)))
      • ## EF (runitor (f,, ff)))
     (psfunctor_runitor EF (f,, ff)))
  (pr2 (runitor (# EF (f,, ff))))
disp_runitor (disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff) =
transportb
  (λ p : # F f · id₁ (F b) ==> # F f,
   disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff ;; id_disp (FF b bb) ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff)
  (psfunctor_runitor F f)
  (((disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff
     ◃◃ disp_psfunctor_id FF bb)
    •• disp_psfunctor_comp FF ff (id_disp bb))
   •• disp_psfunctor_cell FF (disp_runitor ff))

a, b, c, d: B₁
f: B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧
h: B₁ ⟦ c, d ⟧
aa: D₁ a
bb: D₁ b
cc: D₁ c
dd: D₁ d
ff: aa -->[ f] bb
gg: bb -->[ g] cc
hh: cc -->[ h] dd

  ◃◃ disp_psfunctor_comp FF gg hh)
 •• disp_psfunctor_comp FF ff (gg ;; hh))
•• disp_psfunctor_cell FF (disp_lassociator ff gg hh) =

                                          FF hh)%mor_disp ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FF
        ((ff ;; gg)%mor_disp ;; hh))

      (disp_psfunctor_mor FF gg)
      (disp_psfunctor_mor FF hh)
    •• (disp_psfunctor_comp FF ff gg
        ▹▹ disp_psfunctor_mor FF hh))
   •• disp_psfunctor_comp FF (ff ;; gg) hh)

      • psfunctor_comp EF ((f,, ff) · (g,, gg))
          (h,, hh))
     (psfunctor_lassociator EF (f,, ff) (g,, gg)
        (h,, hh)))
  (pr2
     (((# EF (f,, ff)
        ◃ psfunctor_comp EF (g,, gg) (h,, hh))
       • psfunctor_comp EF (f,, ff)
           ((g,, gg) · (h,, hh)))
      • ## EF
          (lassociator (f,, ff) (g,, gg) (h,, hh))))
transportb
  (λ p : # F f · (# F g · # F h) ==> # F (f · g · h),
   disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff ;; (disp_psfunctor_mor FF
                                  gg ;; disp_psfunctor_mor
                                          FF hh)%mor_disp ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FF
        ((ff ;; gg)%mor_disp ;; hh))
  (psfunctor_lassociator F f g h)
  (transportf
     (λ x : pr1
              (# EF (f,, ff)
               · (# EF (g,, gg) · # EF (h,, hh))) ==>
            pr1
              (# EF ((f,, ff) · (g,, gg) · (h,, hh))),
      (λ η : pr1
               (# EF (f,, ff)
                · (# EF (g,, gg) · # EF (h,, hh))) ==>
             pr1
               (# EF ((f,, ff) · (g,, gg) · (h,, hh))),
       pr2
         (# EF (f,, ff)
          · (# EF (g,, gg) · # EF (h,, hh))) ==>[
       η] pr2 (# EF ((f,, ff) · (g,, gg) · (h,, hh))))
        x)
     (base_paths
        (((# EF (f,, ff)
           ◃ psfunctor_comp EF (g,, gg) (h,, hh))
          • psfunctor_comp EF (f,, ff)
              ((g,, gg) · (h,, hh)))
         • ## EF
             (lassociator (f,, ff) (g,, gg) (h,, hh)))
        ((lassociator (# EF (f,, ff)) (# EF (g,, gg))
            (# EF (h,, hh))
          • (psfunctor_comp EF (f,, ff) (g,, gg)
             ▹ # EF (h,, hh)))
         • psfunctor_comp EF ((f,, ff) · (g,, gg))
             (h,, hh))
        (psfunctor_lassociator EF (f,, ff) (g,, gg)
           (h,, hh)))
     (pr2
        (((# EF (f,, ff)
           ◃ psfunctor_comp EF (g,, gg) (h,, hh))
          • psfunctor_comp EF (f,, ff)
              ((g,, gg) · (h,, hh)))
         • ## EF
             (lassociator (f,, ff) (g,, gg) (h,, hh))))) =

  ◃◃ disp_psfunctor_comp FF gg hh)
 •• disp_psfunctor_comp FF ff (gg ;; hh))
•• disp_psfunctor_cell FF (disp_lassociator ff gg hh)

      • psfunctor_comp EF ((f,, ff) · (g,, gg))
          (h,, hh))
     (psfunctor_lassociator EF (f,, ff) (g,, gg)
        (h,, hh)))
  (pr2
     (((# EF (f,, ff)
        ◃ psfunctor_comp EF (g,, gg) (h,, hh))
       • psfunctor_comp EF (f,, ff)
           ((g,, gg) · (h,, hh)))
      • ## EF
          (lassociator (f,, ff) (g,, gg) (h,, hh))))
isaset (# F f · (# F g · # F h) ==> # F (f · g · h))
 apply B₂.

      • ## EF ((η,, ηη) ▹ (g,, gg))))
transportb
  (λ p : # F f1 · # F g ==> # F (f2 · g),
   disp_psfunctor_mor FF ff1 ;; disp_psfunctor_mor FF
                                  gg ==>[
   p] disp_psfunctor_mor FF (ff2 ;; gg))
  (psfunctor_rwhisker F g η)
  ((disp_psfunctor_cell FF ηη
    ▹▹ disp_psfunctor_mor FF gg)
   •• disp_psfunctor_comp FF ff2 gg) = ?b

(** ** Identity *)

Section DispPseudofunctor_identity.

Context {B : bicat} (D : disp_bicat B).


B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
disp_psfunctor_data D D (id_psfunctor B)


B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
disp_psfunctor_data D D (id_psfunctor B)

  
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ x : B, D x → D x
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x y : B) (f : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D x) (yy : D y),
xx -->[ f] yy → ?Goal x xx -->[ f] ?Goal y yy
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x y : B) (f g : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (α : f ==> g)
(xx : D x) (yy : D y) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : xx -->[ g] yy),
ff ==>[ α] gg
→ ?Goal0 x y f xx yy ff ==>[ α] ?Goal0 x y g xx yy gg
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x : B) (xx : D x),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_id (id_psfunctor B) x)
  (id_disp (?Goal x xx))
  (?Goal0 x x (id₁ x) xx xx (id_disp xx))
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x y z : B) (f : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : B ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy : D y) (zz : D z) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : yy -->[ g] zz),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_comp (id_psfunctor B) f g)
  (?Goal0 x y f xx yy ff ;; ?Goal0 y z g yy zz gg)
  (?Goal0 x z (f · g) xx zz (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp)

  
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ x : B, D x → D x
 exact (λ _ y, y).
  
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x y : B) (f : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D x) (yy : D y),
xx -->[ f] yy
→ (λ (x0 : B) (y0 : D x0), y0) x xx -->[
  f] (λ (x0 : B) (y0 : D x0), y0) y yy
 exact (λ _ _ _ _ _ ff, ff).
  
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x y : B) (f g : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (α : f ==> g)
(xx : D x) (yy : D y) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : xx -->[ g] yy),
ff ==>[ α] gg
→ (λ (x0 y0 : B) (f0 : B ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D x0)
   (yy0 : D y0) (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0), ff0) x y f
    xx yy ff ==>[
  α] (λ (x0 y0 : B) (f0 : B ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D x0)
      (yy0 : D y0) (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0), ff0) x y
       g xx yy gg
 exact (λ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ αα, αα).
  
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x : B) (xx : D x),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_id (id_psfunctor B) x)
  (id_disp ((λ (x0 : B) (y : D x0), y) x xx))
  ((λ (x0 y : B) (f : B ⟦ x0, y ⟧) (xx0 : D x0)
    (yy : D y) (ff : xx0 -->[ f] yy), ff) x x (id₁ x)
     xx xx (id_disp xx))
 
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
x: B
xx: D x
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_id (id_psfunctor B) x)
  (id_disp ((λ (x : B) (y : D x), y) x xx))
  ((λ (x y : B) (f : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
    (ff : xx -->[ f] yy), ff) x x (id₁ x) xx xx
     (id_disp xx))
 apply disp_id2_invertible_2cell.
  
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
∏ (x y z : B) (f : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : B ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy : D y) (zz : D z) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : yy -->[ g] zz),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_comp (id_psfunctor B) f g)
  ((λ (x0 y0 : B) (f0 : B ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D x0)
    (yy0 : D y0) (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0), ff0) x y f
     xx yy ff ;; (λ (x0 y0 : B) (f0 : B ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧)
                  (xx0 : D x0) (yy0 : D y0)
                  (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0), ff0) y z g
                   yy zz gg)
  ((λ (x0 y0 : B) (f0 : B ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D x0)
    (yy0 : D y0) (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0), ff0) x z
     (f · g) xx zz (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp)
 
B: bicat
D: disp_bicat B
x, y, z: B
f: B ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: B ⟦ y, z ⟧
xx: D x
yy: D y
zz: D z
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
gg: yy -->[ g] zz
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_comp (id_psfunctor B) f g)
  ((λ (x y : B) (f : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
    (ff : xx -->[ f] yy), ff) x y f xx yy ff ;; (λ 
                                                 (x
                                                 y : B)
                                                 (f : 
                                                 B
                                                 ⟦ x,
                                                 y ⟧)
                                                 (xx : 
                                                 D x)
                                                 (yy : 
                                                 D y)
                                                 (ff : 
                                                 xx -->[
                                                 f] yy),
                                                 ff) y
                                                 z g
                                                 yy zz
                                                 gg)
  ((λ (x y : B) (f : B ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
    (ff : xx -->[ f] yy), ff) x z (f · g) xx zz
     (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp)
 apply disp_id2_invertible_2cell.
Defined.


B: bicat

is_disp_psfunctor D D (id_psfunctor B)
  disp_pseudo_id_data

  disp_pseudo_id_data

  
B: bicat

is_psfunctor
  (total_psfunctor_data D D (id_psfunctor B)
     disp_pseudo_id_data)

  apply id_psfunctor.
Qed.

Definition disp_pseudo_id : disp_psfunctor D D (id_psfunctor B)
  := disp_pseudo_id_data,, disp_pseudo_id_laws.

End DispPseudofunctor_identity.

ff: xx -->[ f] yy
p: φ = ψ
ψψ: ff ==>[ ψ] ff

  (transportb (λ z : f ==> f, ff ==>[ z] ff) p ψψ) =
transportb
  (λ z : # F f ==> # F f,
   disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F (pr1 FF) ff ==>[
   z] disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F (pr1 FF) ff)
  (maponpaths (λ z : f ==> f, ## F z) p)
  (disp_psfunctor_cell D₁ D₂ F (pr1 FF) ψψ)

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F
x, y: B₁
f, g: B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
α: invertible_2cell f g
xx: D₁ x
yy: D₁ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
gg: xx -->[ g] yy
αα: disp_invertible_2cell α ff gg
?Goal •• ?Goal0 =
transportb
  (λ α : # F f ==> # F f,
   disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF ff ==>[
   α] disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF ff)
  (internal_paths_rew (# F f ==> # F f)
     (## F (α • α ^-1))
     (λ p : # F f ==> # F f, p = id₂ (# F f))
     (internal_paths_rew (# F f ==> # F f)
        (## F (id₂ f))
        (λ p : # F f ==> # F f, ## F (α • α ^-1) = p)
        (maponpaths (## F) (vcomp_rinv α))
        (id₂ (# F f)) (psfunctor_id2 F f))
     (## F α • ## F α ^-1) (psfunctor_vcomp F α α ^-1))
  (disp_id2 (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF ff))
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F
x, y: B₁
f, g: B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
α: invertible_2cell f g
xx: D₁ x
yy: D₁ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
gg: xx -->[ g] yy
αα: disp_invertible_2cell α ff gg
?Goal0 •• ?Goal =
transportb
  (λ α : # F g ==> # F g,
   disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF gg ==>[
   α] disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF gg)
  (internal_paths_rew (# F g ==> # F g)
     (## F (α ^-1 • α))
     (λ p : # F g ==> # F g, p = id₂ (# F g))
     (internal_paths_rew (# F g ==> # F g)
        (## F (id₂ g))
        (λ p : # F g ==> # F g, ## F (α ^-1 • α) = p)
        (maponpaths (## F) (vcomp_linv α))
        (id₂ (# F g)) (psfunctor_id2 F g))
     (## F α ^-1 • ## F α) (psfunctor_vcomp F α ^-1 α))
  (disp_id2 (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF gg))

D₁: disp_bicat B₁

 exact (disp_psfunctor_cell _ _ _ FF αα).

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
FF: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F
x, y: B₁

disp_psfunctor_cell D₁ D₂ F FF αα
•• disp_psfunctor_cell D₁ D₂ F FF (disp_inv_cell αα) =
transportb
  (λ α : # F f ==> # F f,
   disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF ff ==>[
   α] disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF ff)
  (internal_paths_rew (# F f ==> # F f)
     (## F (α • α ^-1))
     (λ p : # F f ==> # F f, p = id₂ (# F f))
     (internal_paths_rew (# F f ==> # F f)
        (## F (id₂ f))
        (λ p : # F f ==> # F f, ## F (α • α ^-1) = p)
        (maponpaths (## F) (vcomp_rinv α))
        (id₂ (# F f)) (psfunctor_id2 F f))
     (## F α • ## F α ^-1) (psfunctor_vcomp F α α ^-1))
  (disp_id2 (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF ff))
 abstract
      (rewrite <- (disp_psfunctor_vcomp2_alt _ _ _ _ (pr2 FF));
       rewrite disp_vcomp_rinv;
       rewrite disp_psfunctor_cell_transportb;
       unfold transportb;
       rewrite transport_f_f;
       rewrite (disp_psfunctor_id2 _ _ _ _ (pr2 FF));
       unfold transportb;
       rewrite transport_f_f;
       apply (@transportf_paths _ (λ p, _ ==>[ p ] _));
       apply B₂).

F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
D₁: disp_bicat B₁

•• disp_psfunctor_cell D₁ D₂ F FF αα =

  (λ α : # F g ==> # F g,
   disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF gg ==>[
   α] disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF gg)
  (internal_paths_rew (# F g ==> # F g)

     (## F α ^-1 • ## F α) (psfunctor_vcomp F α ^-1 α))
  (disp_id2 (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F FF gg))
 abstract
      (rewrite <- (disp_psfunctor_vcomp2_alt _ _ _ _ (pr2 FF));
       rewrite disp_vcomp_linv;
       rewrite disp_psfunctor_cell_transportb;
       unfold transportb;
       rewrite transport_f_f;
       rewrite (disp_psfunctor_id2 _ _ _ _ (pr2 FF));
       unfold transportb;

       apply B₂).
Defined.

(** ** Composition *)

Section DispPseudofunctor_comp.

Context {B₁ B₂ B₃ : bicat}
        (F₁ : psfunctor B₁ B₂)
        (F₂ : psfunctor B₂ B₃)
        (D₁ : disp_bicat B₁)
        (D₂ : disp_bicat B₂)
        (D₃ : disp_bicat B₃)
        (FF₁ : disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁)
        (FF₂ : disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂).


B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
disp_psfunctor_data D₁ D₃ (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁)


B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
disp_psfunctor_data D₁ D₃ (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁)

  
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ x : B₁, D₁ x → D₃ (F₂ (F₁ x))
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D₁ x)
(yy : D₁ y),
xx -->[ f] yy
→ ?Goal x xx -->[ # F₂ (# F₁ f)] ?Goal y yy
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x y : B₁) (f g : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (α : f ==> g)
(xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : xx -->[ g] yy),
ff ==>[ α] gg
→ ?Goal0 x y f xx yy ff ==>[
  ## F₂ (## F₁ α)] ?Goal0 x y g xx yy gg
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x : B₁) (xx : D₁ x),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_id (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁) x)
  (id_disp (?Goal x xx))
  (?Goal0 x x (id₁ x) xx xx (id_disp xx))
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x y z : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : B₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y) (zz : D₁ z)
(ff : xx -->[ f] yy) (gg : yy -->[ g] zz),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_comp (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁) f g)
  (?Goal0 x y f xx yy ff ;; ?Goal0 y z g yy zz gg)
  (?Goal0 x z (f · g) xx zz (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp)

  
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ x : B₁, D₁ x → D₃ (F₂ (F₁ x))
 exact (λ x xx, FF₂ _ (FF₁ _ xx)).
  
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D₁ x)
(yy : D₁ y),
xx -->[ f] yy
→ (λ (x0 : B₁) (xx0 : D₁ x0), FF₂ (F₁ x0) (FF₁ x0 xx0))
    x xx -->[
  # F₂ (# F₁ f)] (λ (x0 : B₁) (xx0 : D₁ x0),
                  FF₂ (F₁ x0) (FF₁ x0 xx0)) y yy
 exact (λ x y f xx yy ff, disp_psfunctor_mor _ _ _ FF₂ (disp_psfunctor_mor _ _ _ FF₁ ff)).
  
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x y : B₁) (f g : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (α : f ==> g)
(xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : xx -->[ g] yy),
ff ==>[ α] gg
→ (λ (x0 y0 : B₁) (f0 : B₁ ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D₁ x0)
   (yy0 : D₁ y0) (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0),
   disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
     (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff0)) x y f xx
    yy ff ==>[
  ## F₂ (## F₁ α)] (λ (x0 y0 : B₁)
                    (f0 : B₁ ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D₁ x0)
                    (yy0 : D₁ y0)
                    (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0),
                    disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
                      (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁
                         ff0)) x y g xx yy gg
 exact (λ x y f g α xx yy ff gg αα, disp_psfunctor_cell _ _ _ FF₂ (disp_psfunctor_cell _ _ _ FF₁ αα)).
  
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x : B₁) (xx : D₁ x),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_id (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁) x)
  (id_disp
     ((λ (x0 : B₁) (xx0 : D₁ x0),
       FF₂ (F₁ x0) (FF₁ x0 xx0)) x xx))
  ((λ (x0 y : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x0, y ⟧) (xx0 : D₁ x0)
    (yy : D₁ y) (ff : xx0 -->[ f] yy),
    disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
      (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff)) x x
     (id₁ x) xx xx (id_disp xx))
 
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
x: B₁
xx: D₁ x
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_id (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁) x)
  (id_disp
     ((λ (x : B₁) (xx : D₁ x), FF₂ (F₁ x) (FF₁ x xx))
        x xx))
  ((λ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D₁ x)
    (yy : D₁ y) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy),
    disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
      (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff)) x x
     (id₁ x) xx xx (id_disp xx))

    exact (vcomp_disp_invertible
             (disp_psfunctor_id _ _ _ FF₂ (FF₁ _ xx))
             (disp_psfunctor_invertible_2cell FF₂ (disp_psfunctor_id _ _ _ FF₁ xx))).
  
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
∏ (x y z : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : B₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y) (zz : D₁ z)
(ff : xx -->[ f] yy) (gg : yy -->[ g] zz),
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_comp (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁) f g)
  ((λ (x0 y0 : B₁) (f0 : B₁ ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D₁ x0)
    (yy0 : D₁ y0) (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0),
    disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
      (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff0)) x y f xx
     yy ff ;; (λ (x0 y0 : B₁) (f0 : B₁ ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧)
               (xx0 : D₁ x0) (yy0 : D₁ y0)
               (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0),
               disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
                 (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff0))
                y z g yy zz gg)
  ((λ (x0 y0 : B₁) (f0 : B₁ ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) (xx0 : D₁ x0)
    (yy0 : D₁ y0) (ff0 : xx0 -->[ f0] yy0),
    disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
      (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff0)) x z
     (f · g) xx zz (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp)
 
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat
F₁: psfunctor B₁ B₂
F₂: psfunctor B₂ B₃
D₁: disp_bicat B₁
D₂: disp_bicat B₂
D₃: disp_bicat B₃
FF₁: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ F₁
FF₂: disp_psfunctor D₂ D₃ F₂
x, y, z: B₁
f: B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: B₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧
xx: D₁ x
yy: D₁ y
zz: D₁ z
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
gg: yy -->[ g] zz
disp_invertible_2cell
  (psfunctor_comp (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁) f g)
  ((λ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D₁ x)
    (yy : D₁ y) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy),
    disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
      (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff)) x y f xx
     yy ff ;; (λ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧)
               (xx : D₁ x) (yy : D₁ y)
               (ff : xx -->[ f] yy),
               disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
                 (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff))
                y z g yy zz gg)
  ((λ (x y : B₁) (f : B₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧) (xx : D₁ x)
    (yy : D₁ y) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy),
    disp_psfunctor_mor D₂ D₃ F₂ FF₂
      (disp_psfunctor_mor D₁ D₂ F₁ FF₁ ff)) x z
     (f · g) xx zz (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp)

    exact (vcomp_disp_invertible
             (disp_psfunctor_comp _ _ _ FF₂
                                  (disp_psfunctor_mor _ _ _ FF₁ ff)
                                  (disp_psfunctor_mor _ _ _ FF₁ gg))
             (disp_psfunctor_invertible_2cell FF₂ (disp_psfunctor_comp _ _ _ FF₁ ff gg))).
Defined.

  disp_pseudo_comp_data

  disp_pseudo_comp_data

  
B₁, B₂, B₃: bicat

D₃: disp_bicat B₃

is_psfunctor
  (total_psfunctor_data D₁ D₃ (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁)
     disp_pseudo_comp_data)

  apply (comp_psfunctor (total_psfunctor _ _ _ FF₂) (total_psfunctor _ _ _ FF₁)).
Qed.

Definition disp_pseudo_comp : disp_psfunctor _ _ (comp_psfunctor F₂ F₁)
  := disp_pseudo_comp_data,, disp_pseudo_comp_laws.

End DispPseudofunctor_comp.

(** Fiber of a pseudofunctor *)

C: bicat
HC: is_univalent_2_1 C
D₁, D₂: disp_bicat C
F: disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ (id_psfunctor C)
x, y: C
f, g: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D₁ x
yy: D₁ y
ff: xx -->[ f] yy
p: g = f
transportb (mor_disp ((pr11 F) x xx) ((pr11 F) y yy))
  p ((pr121 F) x y f xx yy ff) =
(pr121 F) x y g xx yy
  (transportb (mor_disp xx yy) p ff)

  (idpath g) ((pr121 F) x y g xx yy ff) =

  apply idpath.
Defined.

End FiberOfFunctor.

Definition disp_psfunctor_id_on_disp_adjequiv
           {B : bicat}
           {D₁ D₂ : disp_bicat B}
           (FF : disp_psfunctor D₁ D₂ (id_psfunctor _))
           {x y : B}
           {f : adjoint_equivalence x y}
           {xx : D₁ x}
           {yy : D₁ y}
           {ff : xx -->[ f ] yy}
           (Hff : disp_left_adjoint_equivalence f ff)
  : disp_left_adjoint_equivalence _ (disp_psfunctor_mor _ _ _ FF ff)
  := pr2 (left_adjoint_equivalence_total_disp_weq
            _ _
            (psfunctor_preserves_adjequiv'
               (total_psfunctor _ _ _ FF)
               (invmap (left_adjoint_equivalence_total_disp_weq f ff) (pr2 f ,, Hff)))).

Notation "♯ FF" := (disp_psfunctor_mor _ _ _ FF) (at level 3) : bicategory_scope.
Notation "♯♯ FF" := (disp_psfunctor_cell _ _ _ FF) (at level 3) : bicategory_scope.
